   vyākhyānaṃ vihitaṃ yāvadupalabdhasya sārataḥ //	vyAKyAnam vihitam yAvat upalabDasya sArataH //
   iti śrīnāgapurī (tirunāṅgūra) divyadeśābhijanena	iti SrI nAgapurI (tiH unA aFgUra) divya deSa aBijanena
   prativādibhayaṅkarācāryāṃnvayabhūṣaṇavidvadvarya	prativAdi BayaFkara AcAryAMnvaya BUzaNa vidvat varya
   śrīkṛṣṇamācāryākhyācāryavaryaputraratnena	SrI kRzNam AcAryAKya AcArya varya putra ratnena
   catustantrīpārāvārapārīṇadigantaviśrāntakīrti dayāmūrti śrīmadbhāṣyakāradivyavaṃśāvatīrṇa śrībhūtapurīnivāsarasika vidvatsārvabhauma hārīta śrīmadāsūrirāmānujācāryadeśikendracaraṇakamalavarivasyāsamadhigatapadavākyapramāṇatantrahṛdayena	catur tantrI pArAvAra pArINa diS anta viSrAnta kIrti dayA mUrti  SrImat BAzya kAra divya vaMSa avatIrNa  SrIBUta purI nivAsa rasika vidvat sArvaBOm
   śrīvaiṣṇavadāsena pra.bha.aṇṇaṅgarācāryeṇa	SrI vEzNava dAsena pra.Ba.aNNaFgara AcAryeNa
   nyāyavyākaraṇaśiromaṇinobhayavedāntaviduṣā praṇītamātmasiddhervyākhyānaṃ	nyAya vyAkaraNa SiraH maNinA uBaya vedAnta viduzA praNItam Atma sidDeH vyAKyAnam
   siddhāñjanaṃ jayatāt ciram /	sidDAQjanam jayatAt ciram /
